> Rounds value upward. The place represents where in the number we want to perform rounding (0 is the 1s place, 1 is the 10s place, -1 is the tenths place, etc). Performed component-wise.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |value|[real2x3](real2x3.md)| |
> |places|[integer](integer.md)| |
> ```TS:Nada
> function Ceil(value : Real2x3, places : Integer) : Real2x3
> ```

> |places|[integer](integer.md)| |
> |numericalBase|[integer](integer.md)| |
> ```TS:Nada
> function Floor(value : Real4x4, places : Integer, numericalBase : Integer) : Real4x4
> ```

 #  Multiply : [integer2](integer2.md)

 `static`

> Multiplies the two matrices together. Matrix multiplication is in right-to-left order, that is if the matrices represent transformations, then 'the' is applied first followed by 'by'.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |by|[integer2x2](integer2x2.md)| |
> |the|[integer2](integer2.md)| |
> ```TS:Nada
> function Multiply(by : Integer2x2, the : Integer2) : Integer2
> ```

> ``` 


---  
 #  Multiply : [real3x3](real3x3.md)

 `static`

> Multiplies the two matrices together. Matrix multiplication is in right-to-left order, that is if the matrices represent transformations, then 'the' is applied first followed by 'by'.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |by|[real3x4](real3x4.md)| |
> |the|[real4x3](real4x3.md)| |

 #  RotateTowards : [quaternion](quaternion.md)

 `static`

> Rotate a quaternion towards another quaternion changing at most maxRadians.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |p0|[quaternion](quaternion.md)| |
> |p1|[quaternion](quaternion.md)| |
> |maxRadians|[real](real.md)| |

> function Slerp(start : Real3, end : Real3, t : Real) : Real3
> ``` 


---  
 #  SlerpUnnormalized : [real2](real2.md)

 `static`

> Spherical linear interpolation. Used to interpolate between two vectors by the parameter t. This is the 'pure' mathematical Slerp function that works on un-normalized input. This effectively traces along an ellipse defined by the two input vectors.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |start|[real2](real2.md)| |
> |end|[real2](real2.md)| |
> |t|[real](real.md)| |
> ```TS:Nada
> function SlerpUnnormalized(start : Real2, end : Real2, t : Real) : Real2
> ```

---  
 #  ToQuaternion : [quaternion](quaternion.md)

 `static`

> |---|---|---|
> |axis|[real3](real3.md)| |
> |radians|[real](real.md)| |

> ```

> |up|[real3](real3.md)| |

> ```

> |right|[real3](real3.md)| |

 #  Transpose : [boolean2x2](boolean2x2.md)

 `static`

> Returns the transposed matrix. A transposed matrix is one where all rows are turned into columns, i.e. A^T[j][i] = A[i][j]
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |p0|[boolean2x2](boolean2x2.md)| |
> ```TS:Nada
> function Transpose(p0 : Boolean2x2) : Boolean2x2
> ``` 


---

> |p0|[boolean2x3](boolean2x3.md)| |

 #  Truncate : [real](real.md)

 `static`

> Rounds value towards zero. The place represents where in the number we want to perform rounding (0 is the 1s place, 1 is the 10s place, -1 is the tenths place, etc).
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |value|[real](real.md)| |
> |places|[integer](integer.md)| |
> ```TS:Nada
> function Truncate(value : Real, places : Integer) : Real
> ```

> ```TS:Nada
> function Truncate(value : Real4x2, places : Integer, numericalBase : Integer) : Real4x2
> ```

 #  Truncate : [real4x3](real4x3.md)

 `static`

> Rounds value towards zero. Performed component-wise.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |p0|[real4x3](real4x3.md)| |
> ```TS:Nada
> function Truncate(p0 : Real4x3) : Real4x3
> ``` 


---  
 #  Truncate : [real4x3](real4x3.md)

 `static`

> Rounds value towards zero. The place represents where in the number we want to perform rounding (0 is the 1s place, 1 is the 10s place, -1 is the tenths place, etc). Performed component-wise.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |value|[real4x3](real4x3.md)| |
> |places|[integer](integer.md)| |
> ```TS:Nada
> function Truncate(value : Real4x3, places : Integer) : Real4x3
> ```
